function readCookie(name) {
var nameEQ = name + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
var c = ca[i];
while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
}
return null;
}
function setCookie(name, value, expires, path, domain, secure){
cookieStr = name + "=" + escape(value) + "; ";
if(expires){
expires = setExpiration(expires);
cookieStr += "expires=" + expires + "; ";
}
if(path){
cookieStr += "path=" + path + "; ";
}
if(domain){
cookieStr += "domain=" + domain + "; ";
}
if(secure){
cookieStr += "secure; ";
}
document.cookie = cookieStr;
}
function setExpiration(cookieLife){
var today = new Date();
var expr = new Date(today.getTime() + cookieLife * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
return expr.toGMTString();
}
var pageLoadDate = new Date();
var lastActivityDateTime=readCookie('lastActivityDateTime');
var diffVisited;
if(readCookie('lastActivityDateTime')!==null){
diffVisited = pageLoadDate.getTime()-lastActivityDateTime;
inactivePeriod = Math.round(diffVisited / 60000);
if(inactivePeriod>=30){
setCookie('isQualifiedCustomer', '', -1, '/', '');
setCookie('numberOfCustomerViews', '', -1, '/', '');
setCookie('numberOfPdpViews', '', -1, '/', '');
setCookie('lastActivityDateTime', '', -1, '/', '');
}
}
if( readCookie('numberOfCustomerViews')!='' && readCookie('numberOfCustomerViews')!=null){
var pageVisit = readCookie('numberOfCustomerViews');
}else{
var pageVisit=0;
}
if( readCookie('numberOfPdpViews')!='' && readCookie('numberOfPdpViews')!=null){
var pdpPageViews=readCookie("numberOfPdpViews");
} else {
var pdpPageViews=0;
}
setCookie('lastActivityDateTime',pageLoadDate.getTime(),'','/');
if(!(readCookie('isQualifiedCustomer'))||(readCookie('isQualifiedCustomer')==='')){
pageVisit ++;
if(window.location.pathname.indexOf("/property") > -1) {
pdpPageViews++;
}
setCookie("numberOfCustomerViews",pageVisit,'','/');
if(pdpPageViews!=0){
setCookie("numberOfPdpViews", pdpPageViews,'','/');
}
}

}

}

function processVisit(){
if (GA_xmlhttp.readyState == 4) {
try {
data = JSON.parse(GA_xmlhttp.responseText) || '';
if (data && data.processVisitor == "yes") {
ga('set', 'dimension1',data.visitorId );
ga('set', 'dimension2', data.visitCount);
ga('set', 'dimension3',data.lastVisitDate );
ga('set', 'dimension4',data.firstTouch );
ga('set', 'dimension5',data.registeredCustomer );
ga('set','dimension11',data.realbidUserId);
visitorId = data.visitorId;
getCustomDimension(visitorId);
CLIENT_IP_ADDRESS = data.CLIENT_IP_ADDRESS;
window.optimizely = window.optimizely || [];
window.optimizely.push("activateUniversalAnalytics");
}
} catch(err) {
//TODO: Log GA
}
}
}
function getCustomDimension(visitorId){
try{
var dimensionParams = "vstrId=" +visitorId ;
GA_xmldimension.onreadystatechange=setCustomDimension;
if(contextPath.indexOf("portal")>0) {
GA_xmldimension.open("GET",contextPath+"/api/getExperiments?experimentType=onLoad",true);
} else {
GA_xmldimension.open("GET",contextPath+"/portal/api/getExperiments?experimentType=onLoad",true);
}
GA_xmldimension.setRequestHeader("Content-type","application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
GA_xmldimension.send(dimensionParams);
}catch(e){
console.log(e);
}
}
function setCustomDimension(){
try{
if (GA_xmldimension.readyState == 4){

for (x = 0; x < dimensionData.length; x++) {
if(dimensionData[x].isActive == 'true' && dimensionData[x].experimentIndex,dimensionData[x].variation != null && dimensionData[x].experimentIndex,dimensionData[x].variation != 'null' && dimensionData[x].experimentIndex,dimensionData[x].variation != ''){

window._mfq.push(["setVariable", dimensionData[x].experimentKey, dimensionData[x].variation]);
}
}
}
}catch(e){
console.log(e);
}
}

function isActivatePlugin(pageList){
if(pageList == 'ALL'){
return true;
}else{
var pageListArray=[];
pageListArray = pageList.split(',');
for(x = 0; x < pageListArray.length; x++){
var cUrl = window.location.pathname;
if(window.location.pathname == '/' || window.location.pathname == contextPath+'/'){
cUrl='home';
}
if(cUrl.indexOf(pageListArray[x])>-1){
return true;
}
}
return false;
}
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function() {
addAltTag();
});
function addAltTag(){
$('img').each(function(){
var $img = $(this);
var attr = $(this).attr('alt');
if (typeof attr == "undefined" || attr == false) {
var filename = $img.attr('src')
$img.attr('alt', filename.substring(0, filename.lastIndexOf('.')));
}
});
}
</script>
